              <span id="reviewTextContainer2195379645" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14045664593908483858">I don’t know how how to describe what I feel at the end of the book!<br/><br/><br/>I know exactly what I felt at the beginning of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3522419.Nemesis__Harry_Hole___4_' title='Nemesis (Harry Hole, #4) by Jo Nesbø' rel='nofollow noopener'>Nemesis</a> (and through three quarters of the plot): <br/><br/><b>I thought, it was one of the best mystery books I ever read.</b> <br/><br/><br/>And then...the final spurt towards the finishing line...and...my initial sensations about my reading <i>orgasm</i> went rapidly downwards. And, believe or not, I finished it, if not confused, but more conflicted than I'd like to.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484593543ra/21732379.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>The Book#4 in the series is VERY VERY complex. Many </b></span>
  <span id="freeText14045664593908483858" style="display:none">I don’t know how how to describe what I feel at the end of the book!<br><br><br>I know exactly what I felt at the beginning of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3522419.Nemesis__Harry_Hole___4_" title="Nemesis (Harry Hole, #4) by Jo Nesbø" rel="nofollow noopener">Nemesis</a> (and through three quarters of the plot): <br><br><b>I thought, it was one of the best mystery books I ever read.</b> <br><br><br>And then...the final spurt towards the finishing line...and...my initial sensations about my reading <i>orgasm</i> went rapidly downwards. And, believe or not, I finished it, if not confused, but more conflicted than I'd like to.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484593543ra/21732379.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The Book#4 in the series is VERY VERY complex. Many many things happen here. </b><br><br>It has both, advantages and disadvantages. <br><b>
  <u>The goody: </u>
</b>it won’t leave you time to catch a breath, the plot pacing is EXTREMELY fast. <b>
  <u>Less good: </u>
</b>the plot is very scattered and demands a lot of brain work (don't even try to read it at work, between the meetings, very challenging). As a reader, you need to digest A LOT of information, while the focus of the story keeps on changing CONSTANTLY. And toward the end the author intensifies this effect, starting LITERALLY to jump from one scene to another. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489074474ra/22183318.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Strangely enough, but I found it actually pretty refreshing and thrilling, while reading the first 80%, and then, instead of <i>being complex and multilayered</i> the story-line turned into <i>over-complicated and incomprehensible</i>. <br><br>My biggest irritation is the resolving of two running cases. Not the fact that they were resolved, and for sure not the fact that it was Harry who did the whole job (bless him!), but the way the perpetrators scheduled their plans (REALLY?!), and a very <s>weird</s> extravagant WAY to fulfill their plans. Very confusing, utterly improbable and very <i>soap-opera-like</i>.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Self-staging suicide was my biggest problem. I don't buy it. No way. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>
  <u>The final thoughts:</u>
</b><br><br>Jo Nesbo is a very talented author, and he is getting better and better with every installment. It is just so...I have very high exceptions for his works, maybe I became a bit more critical and a bit less reasonable and a bit more bitchy and a bit less logical, but it was 10 stars for me for the first half of the book, and not more than 3 towards the end. <br><br>I can't wait to read the next sequel though. Does it explain my critical mood?!<br><br><br><br><br><br><i>***And of course I want to read it only with my girls! BR with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2179183716" rel="nofollow noopener">Sofia </a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2180190468?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Alona</a></i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6660160256883610830">There are mysteries, there are thrillers and then there is the best of both worlds called Jo Nesbo books. I am officially a fan after Nemesis!<br/><br/>Harry Hole is part of a joint investigation with Robbery department of a bank robbery gone wrong. When the escalations in robberies happen with more daring savagery, Hole starts a parallel investigation with Boete (wonderkid) and an extremely well connected gypsy ex-robber doing time playing mind games. <br/><br/>That is just the beginning. He gets a call from a ex-</span>
  <span id="freeText6660160256883610830" style="display:none">There are mysteries, there are thrillers and then there is the best of both worlds called Jo Nesbo books. I am officially a fan after Nemesis!<br /><br />Harry Hole is part of a joint investigation with Robbery department of a bank robbery gone wrong. When the escalations in robberies happen with more daring savagery, Hole starts a parallel investigation with Boete (wonderkid) and an extremely well connected gypsy ex-robber doing time playing mind games. <br /><br />That is just the beginning. He gets a call from a ex-girlfriend and after a date about which he couldn't remember a thing, he discovers her body, which the police close an open and shut suicide. Only Harry starts investigating the murder and finds a lot of missing pieces and emails that taunt him surface. <br /><br />The cat and mouse race, though far fetched, gives you an incredible ride with multiple twists, turns and a psychological exploration into revenge. The mystery is quite brilliant (though I guessed right, and then was made to doubt myself) but the thrill is sufficient to sneak read the book. <br /><br />Picking up the rest of the series this year.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2853415324" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6276451198968123755">Oh, Harry Hole... how I love thee. I have missed you! We have so much to catch up. <br/><br/>I loved the book. The story was great, therefore its shiny stars. Why not five? <i>Hmmk, lemme tell you...</i>the audiobook narrator was absolutely <b>HORRIBLE.</b> Monotone, flat, painful. I almost did not listen to the story because of him. Is this Nesbo's fault? Hmm...maybe. I don't know if authors have a saying on who reads their books or if they listen to them prior to the release. If it was not Nesbo I would have quit and</span>
  <span id="freeText6276451198968123755" style="display:none">Oh, Harry Hole... how I love thee. I have missed you! We have so much to catch up. <br /><br />I loved the book. The story was great, therefore its shiny stars. Why not five? <i>Hmmk, lemme tell you...</i>the audiobook narrator was absolutely <b>HORRIBLE.</b> Monotone, flat, painful. I almost did not listen to the story because of him. Is this Nesbo's fault? Hmm...maybe. I don't know if authors have a saying on who reads their books or if they listen to them prior to the release. If it was not Nesbo I would have quit and DNF. Fire this guy! Give him another job where he doesn't have to torture people with his <b>BORING voice.</b> <br /><br />I am biased toward this series. Nothing objective can come out of my mouth. I'm a fan. This review is just meant to express my torturous experience with the audiobook.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2203948236" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15705104130954888575">Once again I enjoyed reading the adventures of Harry Hole. I liked the twists in the plot but felt the author had too many sub plots. Waaler in the background, crazy ex girlfriends, bank robberies and trying to maintain his relationship while his partner is in Moscow trying to get custody of her child. <br/><br/>To add to the broth we now have a Gypsy Sun Tsu criminal genius who is helping Harry. A night out with ex-girlfriend Anna finds Harry waking up in his apartment with a hangover and no memory of wh</span>
  <span id="freeText15705104130954888575" style="display:none">Once again I enjoyed reading the adventures of Harry Hole. I liked the twists in the plot but felt the author had too many sub plots. Waaler in the background, crazy ex girlfriends, bank robberies and trying to maintain his relationship while his partner is in Moscow trying to get custody of her child. <br /><br />To add to the broth we now have a Gypsy Sun Tsu criminal genius who is helping Harry. A night out with ex-girlfriend Anna finds Harry waking up in his apartment with a hangover and no memory of what happened. Anna is Dead, apparently suicide but it could also be murder and is he the murderer as he remembers nothing of his date. <br /><br />The introduction of Beate who can remember every face she sees is told to us several times! Tom Waaler another cop is also lurking and trying to stay one step ahead of Harry. The original murder victim in a bank robbery which turn out not a series of robberies is resolved and a few cliff hangers to make is keen for the next installment. <br /><br />Although it appears to be heading down the soap opera alley his stories are entertaining and easy to read. Oslo also sounds an interesting city.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AG14IJejIDFTAcYnRntkWXpn2VGCxbLowHhNf9CtPDkIN2+ySV59eFHioAl7IOFWqTDlj513sSRQKp7mjNaiDQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7nF6Fx4unEeOvygt3ZD9HsHo7HKmiZP8OUFuZZ/teBLmK22FwNPBDoxcTgPgy3gREr/QrLk7kDCpE738w5bmJg==')})
  }

//<![CDATA[
      var newTip = new Tip($('bookCover_7145565'), "\n\n  <h2><a class=\"readable bookTitle\" href=\"https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7145565-flaskepost-fra-p?from_choice=false&amp;from_home_module=false\">Flaskepost fra P (Afdeling Q, #3)<\/a><\/h2>\n\n      <div>\n        by <a class=\"authorName\" href=\"/author/show/1734716.Jussi_Adler_Olsen?a=9&amp;origin=related_works\">Jussi Adler-Olsen<\/a>\n      <\/div>\n\n          <div class=\"smallText uitext darkGreyText\">\n            <span class=\"minirating\"><span class=\"stars staticStars notranslate\"><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p3\"><\/span><\/span> 4.02 avg rating &mdash; 30,444 ratings<\/span>            &mdash; published 2009\n          <\/div>\n\n    <div class=\"addBookTipDescription\">\n      \n<span id=\"freeTextContainer13425602003167605796\">I Skotlands yderste ende, helt oppe på politistationen i Wick, havde en grøn, ridset flaske stået i en vindueskarm i ganske, ganske lang tid. Den var lille. Ingen tog notits af den, og ingen bemærkede brevet indeni.\n\nDerfor undrede ingen sig over, hv<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText13425602003167605796\" style=\"display:none\">I Skotlands yderste ende, helt oppe på politistationen i Wick, havde en grøn, ridset flaske stået i en vindueskarm i ganske, ganske lang tid. Den var lille. Ingen tog notits af den, og ingen bemærkede brevet indeni.\n\nDerfor undrede ingen sig over, hvad de halvt udviskede bogstaver HJÆLP mon kunne betyde.\n\nDa politikommissær Carl Mørck ad omveje får overdraget den gamle flaskepost, tror han i første omgang, at det næsten udviskede nødskrig er resultatet af grove drengestreger. Men efterhånden som han og hans assistent Assad får afkodet mere og mere af brevet, går det op for dem, at to store drenge blev bortført engang i halvfemserne, og siden er flaskeposten det eneste livstegn, man har fået fra dem.\nMen hvem er drengene? Hvorfor har deres forældre aldrig meldt dem savnet? <span id="freeTextContainer5218200539695699802">Jo Nesbø is a bestselling Norwegian author and musician. He was born in Oslo and grew up in Molde. Nesbø graduated from the Norwegian School of Economics with a degree in economics. Nesbø is primarily famous for his crime novels about Detective Harry Hole, but he is also the main vocals and songwriter for the Norwegian rock band Di Derre. In 2007 Nesbø also released his first children's book, Dokt</span>
  <span id="freeText5218200539695699802" style="display:none">Jo Nesbø is a bestselling Norwegian author and musician. He was born in Oslo and grew up in Molde. Nesbø graduated from the Norwegian School of Economics with a degree in economics. Nesbø is primarily famous for his crime novels about Detective Harry Hole, but he is also the main vocals and songwriter for the Norwegian rock band Di Derre. In 2007 Nesbø also released his first children's book, Doktor Proktors Prompepulver.<br /><br /><b>Series:</b><br />* <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/51155-harry-hole" rel="nofollow noopener">Harry Hole</a><br />* <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/66741-doktor-proktor" rel="nofollow noopener">Doktor Proktor</a><br /><br />For exclusive content about Jo Nesbø and his books, register for the official fan newsletter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://jonesbo.com/newsletter/">https://jonesbo.com/newsletter/</a></span>

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('bookCover_32775291').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('bookCover_32775291').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_32775291').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
</div>
